				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Nach dir, Herr, verlanget mich, BWV 150 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>7 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1704-07 in Arnstadt
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Nach dir, Herr, verlanget mich
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Unto Thee, O Lord, do I lift up my soul
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="ca">Nach dir</span>; <span title="he">Nach dir, Herr, verlanget mich, רי"ב 150</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Aliases
</th>
<td><span title="tr">Nach dir herr verlanget mich</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>

</li><li> Aria (soprano): Doch bin und bleibe ich vergnügt
</li><li> Chorus: Leite mich in deiner Wahrheit
</li><li> Aria (alto, tenor, bass): Zedern müssen von den Winden
</li><li> Chorus: Meine Augen sehen stets zu dem Herrn
</li><li> Chorale (ciaccona): Meine Tage in dem Leide
</li></ol>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>Not every Baroque choral work is centered around a key (or different halves or portions might be centered around different keys), but this work is definitely in B minor, with one movement in D major and another movement (#6, Meine augen) beginning outside B minor but finding its way there by the closing section.
</p><p>(In Waldersee's full score- haven't checked earlier sources- the bassoon part is notated transposing, in one flat/D minor for most of the work.)
</p><p><br />
</p>
